The expiration is set during key creation in `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go` AddAPIKey() method, which accepts a `SecondsToLive` parameter.\\n\\n### 3. Key Scope and Revocation Enforcement\\n\\nScope enforcement operates at multiple levels:\\n\\n**a) Basic Validation (api_key.go:validateApiKey)**\\n- Checks if key is revoked: `key.IsRevoked != nil && *key.IsRevoked`\\n- Validates organization match: `orgID != key.OrgID`\\n- Ensures key belongs to a service account: `key.ServiceAccountId == nil || *key.ServiceAccountId < 1`\\n\\n**b) Service Account Scope Enforcement (pkg/services/serviceaccounts/models.go)**\\nService accounts have defined scopes:\\n- `ScopeAll = \\\"serviceaccounts:*\\\"` (line 13)\\n- `ScopeID = \\\"serviceaccounts:id:<serviceAccountId>\\\"` (line 14)\\nAnd actions:\\n- `ActionRead = \\\"serviceaccounts:read\\\"` (line 23)\\n- `ActionWrite = \\\"serviceaccounts:write\\\"` (line 24)\\n- `ActionDelete = \\\"serviceaccounts:delete\\\"` (line 26)\\n\\n**c) RBAC Permission Synchronization (pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/rbac_sync.go)**\\nThe `SyncPermissionsHook()` method (line 45) populates permissions for API key identities from the associated service account. Key Retrieval and Database Storage\\n\\n**Modern Token Format (satokengen)**\\n`pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go` implements:\\n- `Decode()` (line 76): Parses prefixed keys in format `gl<serviceId>_<secret>_<checksum>`\\n- Checksum validation for integrity checking\\n- `Hash()` method (line 27): Generates the stored hash of the secret\\n\\n**Legacy Token Format (apikeygen)**\\n`pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go` implements:\\n- `Decode()` and `IsValid()` for legacy base64-encoded API keys\\n\\n**Database Storage (xorm_store.go)**\\n- `GetAPIKeyByHash()` (line 89): Retrieves API key by hashed key from the database\\n- `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate()` (line 103): Updates key usage timestamp for audit trails\\n\\n### 5. Request Handling Chain\\n\\nWhen an API request arrives with an API key:\\n1. `api_key.go:Authenticate()` validates the key\\n2. `validateApiKey()` checks expiration, revocation, org, and service account\\n3. `rbac_sync.go:SyncPermissionsHook()` loads the associated service account's permissions\\n4. `accesscontrol/middleware.go:Middleware()` evaluates final authorization using scopes\\n5. `checker.go` and `evaluator.go` match request against allowed scopes\\n\\nThis multi-layered approach ensures API keys are not only valid and non-expired, but also that each request respects the service account's assigned permissions and organizational scopes.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
